```tsx
/** =========================
 *        Derived Types
 *  ========================= */

type ServiceTypeKey = keyof typeof serviceTypes;
type LevelKey = keyof typeof levels;
type PflegegradKey = keyof typeof pflegegrade;
type RegionKey = keyof typeof regions;
type AgeGroupKey = keyof typeof ageGroups;
type DiagnosisKey = keyof typeof diagnoses;
type SeasonKey = keyof typeof seasons;

type Service = {
  id: number;
  type: ServiceTypeKey;
  hours: number;
  level: LevelKey;
  pflegegrad: PflegegradKey;
  region: RegionKey;
  ageGroup: AgeGroupKey;
  diagnosis: DiagnosisKey;
  season: SeasonKey;
  timeFactors: TimeFactors;
};

type Calculation = {
  baseCost: number;
  socialContributions: number;
  vacationSick: number;
  additionalPayments: number;
  administration: number;
  fixedCosts: number;
  totalCost: number;
  hourlyRate: number;
  adjustedRate: number;
  factors: {
    complexity: number;
    level: number;
    pflegegrad: number;
    region: number;
    age: number;
    diagnosis: number;
    season: number;
  };
};

type ClientInfo = {
  name: string;
  birthDate: string;
  diagnosis: string;
  icfCodes: string;
  address: string;
  id: number | null;
};

type ClientStored = ClientInfo &amp; {
  id: number;
  services: Service[];
  totalCost: number;
  createdAt: string;
  lastModified: string;
};

type Scenario = {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  services: Service[];
  totalCost: number;
  createdAt: string;
};

type SettingsState = {
  autoSave: boolean;
  notifications: boolean;
  defaultRegion: RegionKey;
  currency: &#x27;EUR&#x27;;
  theme: &#x27;light&#x27; | &#x27;dark&#x27;;
};

type Totals = {
  baseCost: number;
  socialContributions: number;
  vacationSick: number;
  additionalPayments: number;
  administration: number;
  fixedCosts: number;
  totalCost: number;
  totalHours: number;
  averageHourlyRate: number;
};

/** =========================
 *       Cost Constants
 *  ========================= */
const SOCIAL_CONTRIB = 0.215;
const VACATION_SICK = 0.342;
const ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS = 0.25;
const FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR = 3.5;
const ADMINISTRATION = 0.10;

/** =========================
 *     Calculation Helpers
 *  ========================= */
const calculateServiceCost = (service: Service): Calculation =&gt; {
  const st = serviceTypes[service.type];
  const baseRate = st.baseRate;
  const complexity = st.complexity;
  const levelFactor = levels[service.level].factor;
  const pflegegradFactor = pflegegrade[service.pflegegrad].factor;
  const regionFactor = regions[service.region].factor;
  const ageFactor = ageGroups[service.ageGroup].factor;
  const diagnosisFactor = diagnoses[service.diagnosis].factor;
  const seasonFactor = seasons[service.season].factor;

  const adjustedRate =
    baseRate *
    complexity *
    levelFactor *
    pflegegradFactor *
    regionFactor *
    ageFactor *
    diagnosisFactor *
    seasonFactor;

  const tf = normalizeTimeFactors(service.hours, service.timeFactors);
  const eveningHours = tf.evening;
  const nightHours = tf.night;
  const weekendHours = tf.weekend;
  const holidayHours = tf.holiday;

  const premiumSum = eveningHours + nightHours + weekendHours + holidayHours;
  const regularHours = Math.max(0, service.hours - premiumSum);

  const regularCost = regularHours * adjustedRate;
  const eveningCost = eveningHours * adjustedRate * 1.2;
  const nightCost = nightHours * adjustedRate * 1.5;
  const weekendCost = weekendHours * adjustedRate * 1.2;
  const holidayCost = holidayHours * adjustedRate * 1.5;

  const baseCost = regularCost + eveningCost + nightCost + weekendCost + holidayCost;

  const withSocial = baseCost * (1 + SOCIAL_CONTRIB);
  const withVacation = withSocial * (1 + VACATION_SICK);
  const withAdditional = withVacation * (1 + ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS);
  const withAdmin = withAdditional * (1 + ADMINISTRATION);
  const withFixed = withAdmin + (service.hours * FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR);

  return {
    baseCost,
    socialContributions: baseCost * SOCIAL_CONTRIB,
    vacationSick: withSocial * VACATION_SICK,
    additionalPayments: withVacation * ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS,
    administration: withAdditional * ADMINISTRATION,
    fixedCosts: service.hours * FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR,
    totalCost: withFixed,
    hourlyRate: service.hours &gt; 0 ? withFixed / service.hours : 0,
    adjustedRate,
    factors: {
      complexity,
      level: levelFactor,
      pflegegrad: pflegegradFactor,
      region: regionFactor,
      age: ageFactor,
      diagnosis: diagnosisFactor,
      season: seasonFactor
    }
  };
};

/** =========================
 *        Component
 *  ========================= */

const PersonalBudgetCalculator: React.FC = () =&gt; {
  const [services, setServices] = useState&lt;Service[]&gt;([{
    id: Date.now(),
    type: &#x27;dosug&#x27;,
    hours: 20,
    level: &#x27;mittel&#x27;,
    pflegegrad: &#x27;pg3&#x27;,
    region: &#x27;dresden&#x27;,
    ageGroup: &#x27;adult&#x27;,
    diagnosis: &#x27;physical&#x27;,
    season: &#x27;standard&#x27;,
    timeFactors: { evening: 0, night: 0, weekend: 0, holiday: 0 }
  }]);

  const [totalCalculation, setTotalCalculation] = useState&lt;Totals&gt;({
    baseCost: 0, socialContributions: 0, vacationSick: 0,
    additionalPayments: 0, administration: 0, fixedCosts: 0,
    totalCost: 0, totalHours: 0, averageHourlyRate: 0
  });

  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState&lt;&#x27;calculator&#x27; | &#x27;analytics&#x27; | &#x27;client&#x27; | &#x27;documents&#x27; | &#x27;scenarios&#x27; | &#x27;settings&#x27;&gt;(&#x27;calculator&#x27;);
  const [showAdvancedOptions, setShowAdvancedOptions] = useState(false);
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState&lt;Lang&gt;(&#x27;ru&#x27;);

  const [clientInfo, setClientInfo] = useState&lt;ClientInfo&gt;({
    name: &#x27;&#x27;, birthDate: &#x27;&#x27;, diagnosis: &#x27;&#x27;, icfCodes: &#x27;&#x27;, address: &#x27;&#x27;, id: null
  });

  const [clients, setClients] = useState&lt;ClientStored[]&gt;([]);
  const [selectedClient, setSelectedClient] = useState&lt;ClientStored | null&gt;(null);
  const [showClientModal, setShowClientModal] = useState(false);

  const [scenarios, setScenarios] = useState&lt;Scenario[]&gt;([]);
  const [selectedScenario, setSelectedScenario] = useState&lt;Scenario | null&gt;(null);
  const [showScenarioModal, setShowScenarioModal] = useState(false);

  const [settings, setSettings] = useState&lt;SettingsState&gt;({
    autoSave: true, notifications: true, defaultRegion: &#x27;dresden&#x27;, currency: &#x27;EUR&#x27;, theme: &#x27;light&#x27;
  });

  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState&lt;{ id: number; message: string; timestamp: string; read: boolean }[]&gt;([]);

  const t = (key: keyof typeof translations.ru) =&gt; translations[language][key] || key;

  /** Actions */

  const addNotification = (message: string) =&gt; {
    const n = { id: Date.now(), message, timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), read: false };
    setNotifications(prev =&gt; [n, ...prev.slice(0, 9)]);
  };

  const addService = () =&gt; {
    const newService: Service = {
      id: Date.now(),
      type: &#x27;dosug&#x27;,
      hours: 20,
      level: &#x27;mittel&#x27;,
      pflegegrad: &#x27;pg3&#x27;,
      region: settings.defaultRegion,
      ageGroup: &#x27;adult&#x27;,
      diagnosis: &#x27;physical&#x27;,
      season: &#x27;standard&#x27;,
      timeFactors: { evening: 0, night: 0, weekend: 0, holiday: 0 }
    };
    setServices(prev =&gt; [...prev, newService]);
  };

  const removeService = (id: number) =&gt; {
    setServices(prev =&gt; prev.filter(s =&gt; s.id !== id));
  };

  const updateService = &lt;K extends keyof Service&gt;(id: number, field: K, value: Service[K]) =&gt; {
    setServices(prev =&gt;
      prev.map(s =&gt; (s.id === id ? { ...s, [field]: value } : s))
    );
  };

  const updateTimeFactor = (id: number, factor: keyof TimeFactors, value: number) =&gt; {
    setServices(prev =&gt;
      prev.map(s =&gt; {
        if (s.id !== id) return s;
        const nextTF = { ...s.timeFactors, [factor]: Math.max(0, Math.min(value, s.hours)) };
        const norm = normalizeTimeFactors(s.hours, nextTF);
        return { ...s, timeFactors: norm };
      })
    );
  };

  const saveClient = () =&gt; {
    const newClient: ClientStored = {
      ...clientInfo,
      id: Date.now(),
      services: [...services],
      totalCost: totalCalculation.totalCost,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      lastModified: new Date().toISOString()
    } as ClientStored;

    setClients(prev =&gt; [...prev, newClient]);
    setClientInfo(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, id: newClient.id }));

    if (settings.notifications) addNotification(`Клиент ${newClient.name} сохранен`);
  };

  const loadClient = (client: ClientStored) =&gt; {
    setClientInfo(client);
    setServices(client.services || []);
    setSelectedClient(client);
    if (settings.notifications) addNotification(`Загружен клиент: ${client.name}`);
  };

  const saveScenario = (name: string) =&gt; {
    const newScenario: Scenario = {
      id: Date.now(),
      name,
      services: [...services],
      totalCost: totalCalculation.totalCost,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    setScenarios(prev =&gt; [...prev, newScenario]);
    if (settings.notifications) addNotification(`Сценарий &quot;${name}&quot; сохранен`);
  };

  const loadTemplate = (templateKey: keyof typeof serviceTemplates) =&gt; {
    const template = serviceTemplates[templateKey];
    const newServices: Service[] = template.services.map((svc, idx) =&gt; ({
      id: Date.now() + idx,
      type: svc.type as ServiceTypeKey,
      hours: svc.hours,
      level: svc.level as LevelKey,
      pflegegrad: svc.pflegegrad as PflegegradKey,
      region: settings.defaultRegion,
      ageGroup: &#x27;adult&#x27;,
      diagnosis: &#x27;physical&#x27;,
      season: &#x27;standard&#x27;,
      timeFactors: { evening: 0, night: 0, weekend: 0, holiday: 0 }
    }));
    setServices(newServices);
    if (settings.notifications) addNotification(`Загружен шаблон: ${template.name[language]}`);
  };

  const copyToClipboard = async (text: string) =&gt; {
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
      addNotification(&#x27;Скопировано в буфер обмена&#x27;);
    } catch {
      addNotification(&#x27;Не удалось скопировать — разрешите доступ к буферу&#x27;);
    }
  };

  const exportToCSV = () =&gt; {
    let csv = &#x27;Service,Hours,Level,Pflegegrad,Region,Age,Diagnosis,Season,Total Cost,Hourly Rate\n&#x27;;
    services.forEach(service =&gt; {
      const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
      const regionName = resolveLocalizedName(regions[service.region].name, language);
      const serviceName = serviceTypes[service.type].name[language];
      const levelName = levels[service.level].name[language];
      const ageName = ageGroups[service.ageGroup].name[language];
      const diagName = diagnoses[service.diagnosis].name[language];
      const seasonName = seasons[service.season].name[language];

      csv += `&quot;${serviceName}&quot;,${service.hours},&quot;${levelName}&quot;,&quot;${pflegegrade[service.pflegegrad].name}&quot;,&quot;${regionName}&quot;,&quot;${ageName}&quot;,&quot;${diagName}&quot;,&quot;${seasonName}&quot;,${calc.totalCost.toFixed(2)},${calc.hourlyRate.toFixed(2)}\n`;
    });

    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: &#x27;text/csv&#x27; });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement(&#x27;a&#x27;);
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `personal_budget_${new Date().toISOString().split(&#x27;T&#x27;)[0]}.csv`;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  };

  /** Totals &amp; autosave */
  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    let totalBaseCost = 0,
      totalSocialContributions = 0,
      totalVacationSick = 0,
      totalAdditionalPayments = 0,
      totalAdministration = 0,
      totalFixedCosts = 0,
      totalCost = 0,
      totalHours = 0;

    for (const s of services) {
      const calc = calculateServiceCost(s);
      totalBaseCost += calc.baseCost;
      totalSocialContributions += calc.socialContributions;
      totalVacationSick += calc.vacationSick;
      totalAdditionalPayments += calc.additionalPayments;
      totalAdministration += calc.administration;
      totalFixedCosts += calc.fixedCosts;
      totalCost += calc.totalCost;
      totalHours += s.hours;
    }

    setTotalCalculation({
      baseCost: totalBaseCost,
      socialContributions: totalSocialContributions,
      vacationSick: totalVacationSick,
      additionalPayments: totalAdditionalPayments,
      administration: totalAdministration,
      fixedCosts: totalFixedCosts,
      totalCost,
      totalHours,
      averageHourlyRate: totalHours &gt; 0 ? totalCost / totalHours : 0
    });

    if (settings.autoSave &amp;&amp; clientInfo.id) {
      const updatedClient: ClientStored = {
        ...(clientInfo as ClientStored),
        services: [...services],
        totalCost,
        lastModified: new Date().toISOString()
      };
      setClients(prev =&gt; prev.map(c =&gt; (c.id === clientInfo.id ? updatedClient : c)));
    }
  }, [services, settings.autoSave, clientInfo.id]);

  /** Projections (для вкладки аналитики) */
  const projections = useMemo(() =&gt; {
    const currentTotal = totalCalculation.totalCost || 0;
    if (!currentTotal) return [] as { year: number; monthlyCost: number; yearlyCost: number; increase: string }[];
    const yearlyTotal = currentTotal * 12;
    const growthRate = 0.055; // 5.5% в год (2.5% инфляция + 3% рост зарплат)
    const arr = [];
    for (let year = 1; year &lt;= 5; year++) {
      const projectedCost = yearlyTotal * Math.pow(1 + growthRate, year);
      arr.push({
        year: new Date().getFullYear() + year,
        monthlyCost: projectedCost / 12,
        yearlyCost: projectedCost,
        increase: (((projectedCost - yearlyTotal) / yearlyTotal) * 100).toFixed(1)
      });
    }
    return arr;
  }, [totalCalculation.totalCost]);

  /** Subcomponents */

  const ProjectionList: React.FC = () =&gt; (
    &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
      &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-xl font-bold mb-4 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
        &lt;TrendingUp className=&quot;mr-2&quot; /&gt;
        5-летний прогноз стоимости
      &lt;/h3&gt;
      &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-3&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 border-b pb-2&quot;&gt;
          &lt;span&gt;Год&lt;/span&gt;
          &lt;span&gt;Месяц&lt;/span&gt;
          &lt;span&gt;Год&lt;/span&gt;
          &lt;span&gt;Рост&lt;/span&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {projections.map((proj, index) =&gt; (
          &lt;div key={index} className=&quot;flex justify-between text-sm&quot;&gt;
            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{proj.year}&lt;/span&gt;
            &lt;span&gt;{formatCurrency(language, proj.monthlyCost)}&lt;/span&gt;
            &lt;span&gt;{formatCurrency(language, proj.yearlyCost)}&lt;/span&gt;
            &lt;span className=&quot;text-red-600&quot;&gt;+{proj.increase}%&lt;/span&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        ))}
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div className=&quot;mt-4 p-3 bg-yellow-50 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
        &lt;p className=&quot;text-xs text-gray-600&quot;&gt;
          Прогноз учитывает инфляцию 2.5% и рост заработной платы 3% в год
        &lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  );

  const ClientModal: React.FC = () =&gt;
    showClientModal ? (
      &lt;div className=&quot;fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl max-w-2xl w-full mx-4 max-h-96 overflow-y-auto&quot;&gt;
          &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-xl font-bold mb-4&quot;&gt;База клиентов&lt;/h3&gt;
          &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-3&quot;&gt;
            {clients.map(client =&gt; (
              &lt;div key={client.id} className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center p-3 border rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                &lt;div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{client.name}&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;
                    {formatCurrency(language, client.totalCost)} / мес | {new Date(client.createdAt).toLocaleDateString(localeByLang[language])}
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;space-x-2&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;button
                    onClick={() =&gt; { loadClient(client); setShowClientModal(false); }}
                    className=&quot;text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800&quot;
                  &gt;
                    Загрузить
                  &lt;/button&gt;
                  &lt;button
                    onClick={() =&gt; setClients(prev =&gt; prev.filter(c =&gt; c.id !== client.id))}
                    className=&quot;text-red-600 hover:text-red-800&quot;
                  &gt;
                    Удалить
                  &lt;/button&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            ))}
          &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-end mt-4 space-x-2&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; setShowClientModal(false)}
              className=&quot;px-4 py-2 bg-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-400&quot;
            &gt;
              Закрыть
            &lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    ) : null;

  const ScenarioModal: React.FC = () =&gt;
    showScenarioModal ? (
      &lt;div className=&quot;fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl max-w-2xl w-full mx-4&quot;&gt;
          &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-xl font-bold mb-4&quot;&gt;Сценарии и шаблоны&lt;/h3&gt;

          &lt;div className=&quot;mb-6&quot;&gt;
            &lt;h4 className=&quot;font-medium mb-3&quot;&gt;Готовые шаблоны:&lt;/h4&gt;
            &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-3&quot;&gt;
              {Object.entries(serviceTemplates).map(([key, template]) =&gt; (
                &lt;button
                  key={key}
                  onClick={() =&gt; { loadTemplate(key as keyof typeof serviceTemplates); setShowScenarioModal(false); }}
                  className=&quot;p-3 border rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-50 text-left&quot;
                &gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{template.name[language]}&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;{template.services.length} услуг&lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/button&gt;
              ))}
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;

          &lt;div&gt;
            &lt;h4 className=&quot;font-medium mb-3&quot;&gt;Сохраненные сценарии:&lt;/h4&gt;
            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-2&quot;&gt;
              {scenarios.map(scenario =&gt; (
                &lt;div key={scenario.id} className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center p-3 border rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{scenario.name}&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;
                      {formatCurrency(language, scenario.totalCost)} | {new Date(scenario.createdAt).toLocaleDateString(localeByLang[language])}
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;space-x-2&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;button
                      onClick={() =&gt; { setServices(scenario.services); setShowScenarioModal(false); }}
                      className=&quot;text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800&quot;
                    &gt;
                      Загрузить
                    &lt;/button&gt;
                    &lt;button
                      onClick={() =&gt; setScenarios(prev =&gt; prev.filter(s =&gt; s.id !== scenario.id))}
                      className=&quot;text-red-600 hover:text-red-800&quot;
                    &gt;
                      Удалить
                    &lt;/button&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              ))}
            &lt;/div&gt;

            &lt;div className=&quot;mt-4&quot;&gt;
              &lt;input
                type=&quot;text&quot;
                placeholder=&quot;Название сценария&quot;
                className=&quot;w-full p-2 border rounded-md&quot;
                onKeyDown={(e) =&gt; {
                  const target = e.currentTarget;
                  if (e.key === &#x27;Enter&#x27; &amp;&amp; target.value.trim()) {
                    saveScenario(target.value.trim());
                    target.value = &#x27;&#x27;;
                  }
                }}
              /&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;

          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-end mt-4&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; setShowScenarioModal(false)}
              className=&quot;px-4 py-2 bg-gray-300 rounded hover:bg-gray-400&quot;
            &gt;
              Закрыть
            &lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    ) : null;

  /** Render */

  return (
    &lt;div className=&quot;max-w-7xl mx-auto p-4 sm:p-6 bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-50 to-indigo-50 min-h-screen&quot;&gt;
      &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white rounded-xl shadow-xl&quot;&gt;
        {/* Header */}
        &lt;div className=&quot;border-b border-gray-200 p-4 flex justify-between items-center&quot;&gt;
          &lt;h1 className=&quot;text-2xl sm:text-3xl font-bold text-gray-800 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
            &lt;Calculator className=&quot;text-blue-600 mr-3&quot; size={32} /&gt;
            &lt;span className=&quot;hidden sm:inline&quot;&gt;Профессиональный калькулятор персонального бюджета&lt;/span&gt;
            &lt;span className=&quot;sm:hidden&quot;&gt;Калькулятор ПБ&lt;/span&gt;
          &lt;/h1&gt;

          &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center space-x-2&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; setLanguage(prev =&gt; (prev === &#x27;ru&#x27; ? &#x27;de&#x27; : &#x27;ru&#x27;))}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-1 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-200&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;Globe size={16} className=&quot;mr-1&quot; /&gt;
              {language.toUpperCase()}
            &lt;/button&gt;

            &lt;div className=&quot;relative&quot;&gt;
              &lt;button className=&quot;p-2 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-lg relative&quot;&gt;
                &lt;Bell size={20} /&gt;
                {notifications.filter(n =&gt; !n.read).length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; (
                  &lt;span className=&quot;absolute -top-1 -right-1 bg-red-500 text-white text-xs rounded-full w-5 h-5 flex items-center justify-center&quot;&gt;
                    {notifications.filter(n =&gt; !n.read).length}
                  &lt;/span&gt;
                )}
              &lt;/button&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;

            &lt;div className=&quot;sm:hidden&quot;&gt;
              &lt;Smartphone size={20} className=&quot;text-blue-600&quot; /&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;

        {/* Nav */}
        &lt;div className=&quot;border-b border-gray-200&quot;&gt;
          &lt;nav className=&quot;flex overflow-x-auto px-6&quot;&gt;
            {([
              { id: &#x27;calculator&#x27;, label: translations[language].calculator, icon: Calculator },
              { id: &#x27;analytics&#x27;, label: translations[language].analytics, icon: BarChart3 },
              { id: &#x27;client&#x27;, label: translations[language].client, icon: Users },
              { id: &#x27;documents&#x27;, label: translations[language].documents, icon: FileText },
              { id: &#x27;scenarios&#x27;, label: translations[language].scenarios, icon: Database },
              { id: &#x27;settings&#x27;, label: translations[language].settings, icon: Settings }
            ] as const).map((tab) =&gt; {
              const Icon = tab.icon;
              return (
                &lt;button
                  key={tab.id}
                  onClick={() =&gt; setActiveTab(tab.id as typeof activeTab)}
                  className={`py-4 px-3 border-b-2 font-medium text-sm whitespace-nowrap ${
                    activeTab === tab.id
                      ? &#x27;border-blue-500 text-blue-600&#x27;
                      : &#x27;border-transparent text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700 hover:border-gray-300&#x27;
                  }`}
                &gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;Icon className=&quot;mr-1 sm:mr-2&quot; size={16} /&gt;
                    &lt;span className=&quot;hidden sm:inline&quot;&gt;{tab.label}&lt;/span&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/button&gt;
              );
            })}
          &lt;/nav&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;div className=&quot;p-4 sm:p-6&quot;&gt;
          {/* Quick actions */}
          &lt;div className=&quot;mb-6 flex flex-wrap gap-2&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={saveClient}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-2 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-green-700 text-sm&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;Save className=&quot;mr-1&quot; size={16} /&gt;
              {translations[language].save}
            &lt;/button&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; setShowClientModal(true)}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 text-sm&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;Database className=&quot;mr-1&quot; size={16} /&gt;
              {translations[language].load}
            &lt;/button&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; setShowScenarioModal(true)}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-2 bg-purple-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-purple-700 text-sm&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;FileText className=&quot;mr-1&quot; size={16} /&gt;
              Шаблоны
            &lt;/button&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={exportToCSV}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-2 bg-orange-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-orange-700 text-sm&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;Download className=&quot;mr-1&quot; size={16} /&gt;
              CSV
            &lt;/button&gt;
            &lt;button
              onClick={() =&gt; copyToClipboard(JSON.stringify({ services, clientInfo, totalCalculation }))}
              className=&quot;flex items-center px-3 py-2 bg-gray-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-700 text-sm&quot;
            &gt;
              &lt;Copy className=&quot;mr-1&quot; size={16} /&gt;
              {translations[language].copy}
            &lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;

          {/* Calculator */}
          {activeTab === &#x27;calculator&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
            &lt;div&gt;
              &lt;div className=&quot;flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center mb-6 gap-4&quot;&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;button
                    onClick={() =&gt; setShowAdvancedOptions(v =&gt; !v)}
                    className=&quot;flex items-center text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800&quot;
                  &gt;
                    {showAdvancedOptions ? &lt;EyeOff size={16} /&gt; : &lt;Eye size={16} /&gt;}
                    &lt;span className=&quot;ml-1&quot;&gt;
                      {showAdvancedOptions ? &#x27;Скрыть&#x27; : &#x27;Показать&#x27;} расширенные опции
                    &lt;/span&gt;
                  &lt;/button&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;

                &lt;div className=&quot;flex gap-2&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;button
                    onClick={addService}
                    className=&quot;flex items-center bg-green-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-green-700 transition-colors&quot;
                  &gt;
                    &lt;Plus className=&quot;mr-2&quot; size={16} /&gt;
                    {translations[language].addService}
                  &lt;/button&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;

              {services.map((service, index) =&gt; {
                const calculation = calculateServiceCost(service);
                return (
                  &lt;div key={service.id} className=&quot;bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-4 sm:p-6 mb-6 border border-gray-200&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center mb-4&quot;&gt;
                      &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-xl font-semibold text-gray-700&quot;&gt;Услуга {index + 1}&lt;/h3&gt;
                      {services.length &gt; 1 &amp;&amp; (
                        &lt;button
                          onClick={() =&gt; removeService(service.id)}
                          className=&quot;text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 p-1&quot;
                        &gt;
                          &lt;Minus size={20} /&gt;
                        &lt;/button&gt;
                      )}
                    &lt;/div&gt;

                    &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-4&quot;&gt;
                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].serviceType}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.type}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;type&#x27;, e.target.value as ServiceTypeKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(serviceTypes).map(([key, type]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{type.name[language]}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                        &lt;div className=&quot;text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1&quot;&gt;
                          {serviceTypes[service.type].sgb}
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].hoursPerMonth}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;input
                          type=&quot;number&quot;
                          value={service.hours}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;hours&#x27;, Math.max(0, parseInt(e.target.value || &#x27;0&#x27;, 10)) as number)}
                          min={0}
                          max={200}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        /&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].icfLevel}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.level}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;level&#x27;, e.target.value as LevelKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(levels).map(([key, level]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{level.name[language]}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;Pflegegrad&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.pflegegrad}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;pflegegrad&#x27;, e.target.value as PflegegradKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(pflegegrade).map(([key, pg]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{pg.name}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].region}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.region}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;region&#x27;, e.target.value as RegionKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(regions).map(([key, region]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;
                              {resolveLocalizedName(region.name, language)}
                            &lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].ageGroup}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.ageGroup}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;ageGroup&#x27;, e.target.value as AgeGroupKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(ageGroups).map(([key, age]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{age.name[language]}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].diagnosis}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.diagnosis}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;diagnosis&#x27;, e.target.value as DiagnosisKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(diagnoses).map(([key, diagnosis]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{diagnosis.name[language]}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;

                      &lt;div&gt;
                        &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{translations[language].seasonalPeriod}&lt;/label&gt;
                        &lt;select
                          value={service.season}
                          onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;season&#x27;, e.target.value as SeasonKey)}
                          className=&quot;w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                        &gt;
                          {Object.entries(seasons).map(([key, season]) =&gt; (
                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;{season.name[language]}&lt;/option&gt;
                          ))}
                        &lt;/select&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;

                    {showAdvancedOptions &amp;&amp; (
                      &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-4 rounded-lg mb-4&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;h4 className=&quot;font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3&quot;&gt;Временные коэффициенты (часы с надбавками)&lt;/h4&gt;
                        &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3&quot;&gt;
                          &lt;div&gt;
                            &lt;label className=&quot;block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;Вечерние (+20%)&lt;/label&gt;
                            &lt;input
                              type=&quot;number&quot;
                              value={service.timeFactors.evening}
                              onChange={(e) =&gt; updateTimeFactor(service.id, &#x27;evening&#x27;, parseInt(e.target.value || &#x27;0&#x27;, 10))}
                              min={0}
                              max={service.hours}
                              className=&quot;w-full p-1 text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                            /&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div&gt;
                            &lt;label className=&quot;block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;Ночные (+50%)&lt;/label&gt;
                            &lt;input
                              type=&quot;number&quot;
                              value={service.timeFactors.night}
                              onChange={(e) =&gt; updateTimeFactor(service.id, &#x27;night&#x27;, parseInt(e.target.value || &#x27;0&#x27;, 10))}
                              min={0}
                              max={service.hours}
                              className=&quot;w-full p-1 text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                            /&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div&gt;
                            &lt;label className=&quot;block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;Выходные (+20%)&lt;/label&gt;
                            &lt;input
                              type=&quot;number&quot;
                              value={service.timeFactors.weekend}
                              onChange={(e) =&gt; updateTimeFactor(service.id, &#x27;weekend&#x27;, parseInt(e.target.value || &#x27;0&#x27;, 10))}
                              min={0}
                              max={service.hours}
                              className=&quot;w-full p-1 text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                            /&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div&gt;
                            &lt;label className=&quot;block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;Праздники (+50%)&lt;/label&gt;
                            &lt;input
                              type=&quot;number&quot;
                              value={service.timeFactors.holiday}
                              onChange={(e) =&gt; updateTimeFactor(service.id, &#x27;holiday&#x27;, parseInt(e.target.value || &#x27;0&#x27;, 10))}
                              min={0}
                              max={service.hours}
                              className=&quot;w-full p-1 text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                            /&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    )}

                    &lt;div className=&quot;bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-50 to-indigo-50 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                      &lt;h4 className=&quot;font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;Euro className=&quot;mr-2&quot; size={16} /&gt;
                        {translations[language].detailedCalculation}
                      &lt;/h4&gt;

                      &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].baseCost}:&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, calculation.baseCost)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].socialContributions} (21,5%):&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, calculation.socialContributions)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].vacationSick} (34,2%):&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, calculation.vacationSick)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].additionalPayments} (25%):&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, calculation.additionalPayments)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].administration} (10%):&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, calculation.administration)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                            &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].fixedCosts}:&lt;/span&gt;
                            &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, calculation.fixedCosts)}&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;border-t pt-3 mt-3&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center&quot;&gt;
                          &lt;span className=&quot;text-lg font-bold&quot;&gt;{translations[language].totalPerMonth}:&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;span className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, calculation.totalCost)}&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center text-sm text-gray-600&quot;&gt;
                          &lt;span&gt;{translations[language].hourlyRate}:&lt;/span&gt;
                          &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, calculation.hourlyRate)}/час&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                );
              })}

              {/* Totals */}
              &lt;div className=&quot;bg-gradient-to-r from-indigo-600 to-blue-600 text-white p-6 rounded-xl&quot;&gt;
                &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold mb-4 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;Clock className=&quot;mr-3&quot; /&gt;
                  {translations[language].totalBudget}
                &lt;/h2&gt;

                &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm opacity-90 mb-1&quot;&gt;Всего часов в месяц&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold&quot;&gt;{totalCalculation.totalHours}&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm opacity-90 mb-1&quot;&gt;Общая стоимость&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.totalCost)}&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm opacity-90 mb-1&quot;&gt;Средняя ставка&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.averageHourlyRate)}/час&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;

                &lt;div className=&quot;mt-6 bg-white bg-opacity-10 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;h3 className=&quot;font-semibold mb-3&quot;&gt;Структура расходов:&lt;/h3&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Базовая стоимость услуг:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.baseCost)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Социальные взносы:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.socialContributions)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Отпуска и больничные:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.vacationSick)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Дополнительные выплаты:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.additionalPayments)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Администрирование:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.administration)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between py-1&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Фиксированные расходы:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;+{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.fixedCosts)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          )}

          {/* Analytics */}
          {activeTab === &#x27;analytics&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-6&quot;&gt;
              &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                &lt;TrendingUp className=&quot;mr-3&quot; /&gt;
                Расширенная аналитика и прогнозирование
              &lt;/h2&gt;

              &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;lg:col-span-2&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;ProjectionList /&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;div&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-xl font-bold mb-4&quot;&gt;Ключевые показатели&lt;/h3&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-3&quot;&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Услуг активно:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span className=&quot;font-bold&quot;&gt;{services.length}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Средний коэффициент:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span className=&quot;font-bold&quot;&gt;
                          {services.length &gt; 0
                            ? (services.reduce((sum, s) =&gt; {
                                const calc = calculateServiceCost(s);
                                const product = Object.values(calc.factors).reduce((a, b) =&gt; a * b, 1);
                                return sum + product;
                              }, 0) / services.length).toFixed(2)
                            : &#x27;0&#x27;}
                        &lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;Годовая стоимость:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span className=&quot;font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;{formatCurrency(language, totalCalculation.totalCost * 12)}&lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                      &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;span&gt;5-летняя стоимость:&lt;/span&gt;
                        &lt;span className=&quot;font-bold text-red-600&quot;&gt;
                          {formatCurrency(language, (totalCalculation.totalCost || 0) * 12 * 5 * 1.31)}
                        &lt;/span&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          )}

          {/* Clients */}
          {activeTab === &#x27;client&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-6&quot;&gt;
              &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                &lt;Users className=&quot;mr-3&quot; /&gt;
                Управление клиентами
              &lt;/h2&gt;

              &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2&quot;&gt;Имя и фамилия&lt;/label&gt;
                    &lt;input
                      type=&quot;text&quot;
                      value={clientInfo.name}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, name: e.target.value }))}
                      className=&quot;w-full p-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                      placeholder=&quot;Иван Иванов&quot;
                    /&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;

                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2&quot;&gt;Дата рождения&lt;/label&gt;
                    &lt;input
                      type=&quot;date&quot;
                      value={clientInfo.birthDate}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, birthDate: e.target.value }))}
                      className=&quot;w-full p-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                    /&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;

                  &lt;div className=&quot;md:col-span-2&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;label className=&quot;block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2&quot;&gt;Основной диагноз&lt;/label&gt;
                    &lt;input
                      type=&quot;text&quot;
                      value={clientInfo.diagnosis}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, diagnosis: e.target.value }))}
                      className=&quot;w-full p-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500&quot;
                      placeholder=&quot;Например: Церебральный паралич&quot;
                    /&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;

              {clients.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; (
                &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Последние клиенты&lt;/h3&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-3&quot;&gt;
                    {clients.slice(-5).map(client =&gt; (
                      &lt;div key={client.id} className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center p-3 border rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;{client.name}&lt;/div&gt;
                          &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;
                            {formatCurrency(language, client.totalCost)}/месяц | {new Date(client.lastModified).toLocaleDateString(localeByLang[language])}
                          &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;/div&gt;
                        &lt;button
                          onClick={() =&gt; loadClient(client)}
                          className=&quot;text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 px-3 py-1 border border-blue-600 rounded hover:bg-blue-50&quot;
                        &gt;
                          Загрузить
                        &lt;/button&gt;
                      &lt;/div&gt;
                    ))}
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              )}
            &lt;/div&gt;
          )}

          {/* Settings */}
          {activeTab === &#x27;settings&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-6&quot;&gt;
              &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                &lt;Settings className=&quot;mr-3&quot; /&gt;
                Настройки приложения
              &lt;/h2&gt;

              &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-4&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center justify-between&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div&gt;
                      &lt;label className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;Автосохранение&lt;/label&gt;
                      &lt;p className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Автоматически сохранять изменения клиента&lt;/p&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;input
                      type=&quot;checkbox&quot;
                      checked={settings.autoSave}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setSettings(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, autoSave: e.target.checked }))}
                      className=&quot;w-4 h-4&quot;
                    /&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;

                  &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center justify-between&quot;&gt;
                    &lt;div&gt;
                      &lt;label className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;Уведомления&lt;/label&gt;
                      &lt;p className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Показывать уведомления о действиях&lt;/p&gt;
                    &lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;input
                      type=&quot;checkbox&quot;
                      checked={true}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setSettings(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, notifications: e.target.checked }))}
                      className=&quot;w-4 h-4&quot;
                    /&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;

                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;label className=&quot;block font-medium mb-2&quot;&gt;Регион по умолчанию&lt;/label&gt;
                    &lt;select
                      value={settings.defaultRegion}
                      onChange={(e) =&gt; setSettings(prev =&gt; ({ ...prev, defaultRegion: e.target.value as RegionKey }))}
                      className=&quot;w-full p-2 border rounded-md&quot;
                    &gt;
                      {Object.entries(regions).map(([key, region]) =&gt; (
                        &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;
                          {resolveLocalizedName(region.name, language)}
                        &lt;/option&gt;
                      ))}
                    &lt;/select&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;

              &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white p-6 rounded-xl shadow-lg&quot;&gt;
                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Статистика использования&lt;/h3&gt;
                &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 text-center&quot;&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;{clients.length}&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Клиентов&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-green-600&quot;&gt;{scenarios.length}&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Сценариев&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-purple-600&quot;&gt;{services.length}&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Активных услуг&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-orange-600&quot;&gt;{notifications.length}&lt;/div&gt;
                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-500&quot;&gt;Уведомлений&lt;/div&gt;
                  &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          )}
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;

      {/* Modals */}
      &lt;ClientModal /&gt;
      &lt;ScenarioModal /&gt;

      {/* Notifications */}
      {notifications.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; settings.notifications &amp;&amp; (
        &lt;div className=&quot;fixed bottom-4 right-4 max-w-sm&quot;&gt;
          {notifications.slice(0, 3).map(notification =&gt; (
            &lt;div key={notification.id} className=&quot;bg-blue-600 text-white p-3 rounded-lg shadow-lg mb-2&quot;&gt;
              &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm&quot;&gt;{notification.message}&lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;div className=&quot;text-xs opacity-75&quot;&gt;
                {new Date(notification.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString(localeByLang[language])}
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          ))}
        &lt;/div&gt;
      )}
    &lt;/div&gt;
  );
};

export default PersonalBudgetCalculator;
```

Нужно разделить по файлам (`types.ts`, `constants.ts`, `utils.ts`) или добавить сохранение клиентов/сценариев/настроек в `localStorage`? Скажете — пришлю готовую разбивку.

--- ПОЛЬЗОВАТЕЛЬ ---
Что это даст

--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
Коротко: новый **TSX-файл** делает калькулятор точнее, стабильнее и удобнее развивать. Что именно вы выигрываете:

---

## 1) Точность расчётов
- **Нормализация “надбавочных” часов** (вечер/ночь/выходные/праздники): их сумма никогда не превысит `hours`.  
  → Больше нет завышенных итогов из-за двойного учёта.
- **Все факторы в формуле**: учитываются `Pflegegrad`, возрастная группа, диагноз, сезон, регион, сложность услуги.  
  → Бюджет ближе к реальности и требованиям контролёров.
- **Защита от деления на ноль**: при `hours=0` ставка не превращается в `Infinity/NaN`.

## 2) Надёжность приложения
- **Функциональные обновления состояния** (`setState(prev =&gt; ...)`) для уведомлений/автосохранения.  
  → Нет «гонок» и потери данных при быстром вводе.
- **Автосохранение клиента** обновляет ровно ту запись, которая открыта.

## 3) Корректные выгрузки и локализация
- **CSV без `[object Object]`**: локализованные названия (регион, диагноз и т.д.) выгружаются строками.
- **Формат валют/дат по RU/DE** через `Intl`.  
  → Документы и цифры выглядят профессионально для обеих аудиторий.

## 4) Поддерживаемость и масштабирование
- **Строгая типизация (TypeScript)**:  
  — фиксирует допустимые значения (`keyof typeof ...`),  
  — ловит опечатки и несоответствия на сборке,  
  — IDE показывает подсказки по полям/константам.  
  → Быстрее ревью, меньше регрессий при добавлении новых услуг/коэффициентов.
- **Константы/словари как `as const`**: легче расширять модель (новые услуги, регионы, правила расчётов).

## 5) Прозрачность для пользователя и проверок
- **Детализация структуры затрат** (база, соцвзносы, отпуск/больничные, доплаты, администрирование, фикс-расходы).  
  → Проще обосновывать смету (напр. по SGB IX) и проходить согласование.

## 6) Удобство и UX
- **Шаблоны сценариев** + **быстрые действия** (копия/экспорт/загрузка) → меньше рутинных кликов.
- **Прогноз на 5 лет**: мгновенная оценка долгосрочной нагрузки бюджета (инфляция+зарплаты).

---

### Практический эффект
- **Снижение ошибок** в расчётах и экспортируемых файлах.  
- **Меньше ручных правок** и «случайных» багов из-за типов/опечаток.  
- **Готовность к росту** (добавите новый регион/правило — не сломаете существующее).

---

### Что можно добавить дальше (по желанию)
1) Сохранение клиентов/настроек в `localStorage`/IndexedDB.  
2) Печать/экспорт в PDF с фирменным шаблоном.  
3) Единые модульные тесты на формулу (`calculateServiceCost`) с контрольными кейсами.  
4) Разнести код на модули: `constants.ts`, `types.ts`, `calc.ts`, `i18n.ts`.

--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
Отличный выбор. Добавление **(1) сохранения данных в браузере**, **(3) модульных тестов** и **(4) разбиения кода на модули** даст заметные плюсы по надёжности, удобству и поддерживаемости. Коротко — что именно изменится/улучшится и что нового появится.

---

## 1) Сохранение данных (localStorage / IndexedDB)

**Что появится для пользователя**
- **Автовосстановление сессии:** клиенты/сценарии/настройки остаются после перезагрузки.
- **Резервные копии:** кнопки *Экспорт/Импорт* одним файлом (JSON).
- **Индикатор «Сохранено … сек назад»** и кнопка *Сбросить данные*.
- **Офлайн-режим:** всё работает без сети.

**Технические плюсы**
- Меньше риска потерять изменения.
- Можно хранить достаточно большие базы (IndexedDB предпочтительнее при росте).

**Мини-встраивание**
- При старте: загрузка из хранилища.
- При изменениях: дебаунс-сохранение.
- Версионирование схемы для будущих миграций.

```ts
// storage.ts
export const loadJSON = &lt;T&gt;(k: string, fallback: T): T =&gt; {
  try { const v = localStorage.getItem(k); return v ? JSON.parse(v) as T : fallback; }
  catch { return fallback; }
};
export const saveJSON = (k: string, v: unknown) =&gt; {
  try { localStorage.setItem(k, JSON.stringify(v)); } catch {}
};
```

```ts
// в компоненте
useEffect(() =&gt; {
  setClients(loadJSON(&#x27;pbc.clients&#x27;, []));
  setScenarios(loadJSON(&#x27;pbc.scenarios&#x27;, []));
  setSettings(loadJSON(&#x27;pbc.settings&#x27;, settings =&gt; settings)); // можно через fallback
  // ...
}, []);

useEffect(() =&gt; { const id = setTimeout(() =&gt; saveJSON(&#x27;pbc.clients&#x27;, clients), 400); return () =&gt; clearTimeout(id); }, [clients]);
useEffect(() =&gt; { const id = setTimeout(() =&gt; saveJSON(&#x27;pbc.scenarios&#x27;, scenarios), 400); return () =&gt; clearTimeout(id); }, [scenarios]);
useEffect(() =&gt; { const id = setTimeout(() =&gt; saveJSON(&#x27;pbc.settings&#x27;, settings), 400); return () =&gt; clearTimeout(id); }, [settings]);
```

&gt; Если база начнёт расти (десятки тысяч записей/файлы), переключим хранилище на **IndexedDB** (через `idb`), интерфейс останется прежним.

---

## 3) Тесты (Vitest/Jest) для расчётов и хелперов

**Что появится для команды**
- **Гарантии против регрессий:** любые будущие правки формулы мгновенно ловятся.
- **Документированные «эталонные» кейсы** (golden tests) для расчётов.
- **Покрытие краёв:** `hours=0`, сумма надбавок &gt; `hours`, максимальные коэффициенты.

**Мини-набор тестов**
- 6–10 тестов на `calculateServiceCost()` + 3–4 на `normalizeTimeFactors()`.

```ts
// calc.test.ts (Vitest)
import { describe, it, expect } from &#x27;vitest&#x27;;
import { calculateServiceCost } from &#x27;./calc&#x27;;
import { mkService } from &#x27;./test-utils&#x27;;

describe(&#x27;calculateServiceCost&#x27;, () =&gt; {
  it(&#x27;guards against division by zero&#x27;, () =&gt; {
    const svc = mkService({ hours: 0 });
    const r = calculateServiceCost(svc);
    expect(r.hourlyRate).toBe(0);
  });

  it(&#x27;normalizes premium hours when sum &gt; hours&#x27;, () =&gt; {
    const svc = mkService({ hours: 20, timeFactors: { evening: 10, night: 10, weekend: 10, holiday: 10 } });
    const r = calculateServiceCost(svc);
    expect(r.baseCost).toBeGreaterThan(0);
    // косвенно проверяем: нет превышения и нет NaN
    expect(Number.isFinite(r.totalCost)).toBe(true);
  });

  it(&#x27;applies all factors (region/pg/age/diagnosis/season/complexity)&#x27;, () =&gt; {
    const base = calculateServiceCost(mkService());
    const hi = calculateServiceCost(mkService({
      type: &#x27;assistenz&#x27;, level: &#x27;hoch&#x27;, pflegegrad: &#x27;pg5&#x27;,
      region: &#x27;muenchen&#x27;, ageGroup: &#x27;senior&#x27;, diagnosis: &#x27;neurological&#x27;, season: &#x27;winter&#x27;
    }));
    expect(hi.totalCost).toBeGreaterThan(base.totalCost);
  });
});
```

---

## 4) Разбиение на модули (структура проекта)

**Что появится для разработчиков**
- Чёткая архитектура, понятная навигация, меньше «божественного» компонента.
- Проще тестировать и переиспользовать функции.
- Легче работать в команде (меньше конфликтов в одном файле).

**Предлагаемая структура**
```
/src
  /features/pbc
    calc.ts          // calculateServiceCost, normalizeTimeFactors
    constants.ts     // serviceTypes, levels, regions, ...
    types.ts         // типы Service, Calculation, Totals, ...
    i18n.ts          // translations, helpers formatCurrency/resolveLocalizedName
    storage.ts       // loadJSON/saveJSON, (позже: IndexedDB)
    components/
      PersonalBudgetCalculator.tsx
      ProjectionList.tsx
      ClientModal.tsx
      ScenarioModal.tsx
    __tests__/
      calc.test.ts
      normalizeTimeFactors.test.ts
```

**Технические плюсы**
- **Tree-shaking**: лишнее не попадёт в бандл.
- **Автодополнение/типобезопасность** везде.
- Тесты импортируют только нужные модули (быстрее, изолированнее).

---

## Итого — что изменится и какие новые возможности появятся

- **Надёжность данных**: ничего не теряется при перезагрузке; можно импортировать/экспортировать базу.
- **Качество расчётов** подтверждено тестами; правки формулы не «ломают» прод.
- **Поддерживаемость**: код разбит на логичные части, легче добавлять новые услуги/регионы/правила и выпускать обновления.
- **Готовность к росту**: при увеличении объёма данных просто переключаемся на IndexedDB, тесты остаются теми же.

Отлично. Ниже — готовая разбивка по файлам для **п.1 (локальное сохранение)** и **п.4 (модули)**. Это **чистый TS/React**, без AI-частей. Включены: автозагрузка/автосохранение в `localStorage`, кнопки **Экспорт / Импорт / Сброс**, нормализация надбавочных часов, полный расчёт, i18n и аккуратное форматирование валют/дат.

```

  features/pbc/
    calc.ts
    constants.ts
    i18n.ts
    storage.ts
    types.ts
    components/
      PersonalBudgetCalculator.tsx
```

## `src/features/pbc/types.ts`
```ts
export type Lang = &#x27;ru&#x27; | &#x27;de&#x27;;
export type Localized = Record&lt;Lang, string&gt;;

export type TimeFactors = {
  evening: number;
  night: number;
  weekend: number;
  holiday: number;
};

export type ServiceTypeKey = &#x27;dosug&#x27; | &#x27;haushalt&#x27; | &#x27;begleitung&#x27; | &#x27;assistenz&#x27; | &#x27;pflege&#x27; | &#x27;therapie&#x27; | &#x27;kommunikation&#x27; | &#x27;mobilitaet&#x27; | &#x27;wohnen&#x27;;
export type LevelKey = &#x27;minimal&#x27; | &#x27;basic&#x27; | &#x27;mittel&#x27; | &#x27;hoch&#x27; | &#x27;maximal&#x27;;
export type PflegegradKey = &#x27;pg1&#x27; | &#x27;pg2&#x27; | &#x27;pg3&#x27; | &#x27;pg4&#x27; | &#x27;pg5&#x27;;
export type RegionKey = &#x27;muenchen&#x27; | &#x27;frankfurt&#x27; | &#x27;berlin&#x27; | &#x27;hamburg&#x27; | &#x27;stuttgart&#x27; | &#x27;dresden&#x27; | &#x27;leipzig&#x27; | &#x27;rural&#x27;;
export type AgeGroupKey = &#x27;child&#x27; | &#x27;teen&#x27; | &#x27;adult&#x27; | &#x27;senior&#x27;;
export type DiagnosisKey = &#x27;physical&#x27; | &#x27;visual&#x27; | &#x27;hearing&#x27; | &#x27;cognitive&#x27; | &#x27;psychiatric&#x27; | &#x27;neurological&#x27; | &#x27;multiple&#x27; | &#x27;autism&#x27; | &#x27;intellectual&#x27;;
export type SeasonKey = &#x27;standard&#x27; | &#x27;summer&#x27; | &#x27;winter&#x27; | &#x27;spring&#x27; | &#x27;autumn&#x27;;

export type Service = {
  id: number;
  type: ServiceTypeKey;
  hours: number;
  level: LevelKey;
  pflegegrad: PflegegradKey;
  region: RegionKey;
  ageGroup: AgeGroupKey;
  diagnosis: DiagnosisKey;
  season: SeasonKey;
  timeFactors: TimeFactors;
};

export type Calculation = {
  baseCost: number;
  socialContributions: number;
  vacationSick: number;
  additionalPayments: number;
  administration: number;
  fixedCosts: number;
  totalCost: number;
  hourlyRate: number;
  adjustedRate: number;
  factors: {
    complexity: number;
    level: number;
    pflegegrad: number;
    region: number;
    age: number;
    diagnosis: number;
    season: number;
  };
};

export type Totals = {
  baseCost: number;
  socialContributions: number;
  vacationSick: number;
  additionalPayments: number;
  administration: number;
  fixedCosts: number;
  totalCost: number;
  totalHours: number;
  averageHourlyRate: number;
};

export type ClientInfo = {
  name: string;
  birthDate: string;
  diagnosis: string;
  icfCodes: string;
  address: string;
  id: number | null;
};

export type ClientStored = ClientInfo &amp; {
  id: number;
  services: Service[];
  totalCost: number;
  createdAt: string;
  lastModified: string;
};

export type Scenario = {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  services: Service[];
  totalCost: number;
  createdAt: string;
};

export type SettingsState = {
  autoSave: boolean;
  notifications: boolean;
  defaultRegion: RegionKey;
  currency: &#x27;EUR&#x27;;
  theme: &#x27;light&#x27; | &#x27;dark&#x27;;
};
```

## `src/features/pbc/calc.ts`
```ts
import {
  ADMINISTRATION, ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS, FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR, SOCIAL_CONTRIB,
  VACATION_SICK, ageGroups, diagnoses, levels, pflegegrade, regions, seasons, serviceTypes
} from &#x27;./constants&#x27;;
import type { Calculation, Service, TimeFactors } from &#x27;./types&#x27;;

export const normalizeTimeFactors = (hours: number, tf?: Partial&lt;TimeFactors&gt;): TimeFactors =&gt; {
  const evening = Math.max(0, Math.min(tf?.evening ?? 0, hours));
  const night = Math.max(0, Math.min(tf?.night ?? 0, hours));
  const weekend = Math.max(0, Math.min(tf?.weekend ?? 0, hours));
  const holiday = Math.max(0, Math.min(tf?.holiday ?? 0, hours));
  const sum = evening + night + weekend + holiday;
  if (sum === 0 || sum &lt;= hours) return { evening, night, weekend, holiday };
  const k = hours / sum;
  return {
    evening: Math.floor(evening * k),
    night: Math.floor(night * k),
    weekend: Math.floor(weekend * k),
    holiday: Math.floor(holiday * k),
  };
};

export const calculateServiceCost = (service: Service): Calculation =&gt; {
  const st = serviceTypes[service.type];
  const baseRate = st.baseRate;
  const complexity = st.complexity;
  const levelFactor = levels[service.level].factor;
  const pflegegradFactor = pflegegrade[service.pflegegrad].factor;
  const regionFactor = regions[service.region].factor;
  const ageFactor = ageGroups[service.ageGroup].factor;
  const diagnosisFactor = diagnoses[service.diagnosis].factor;
  const seasonFactor = seasons[service.season].factor;

  const adjustedRate =
    baseRate *
    complexity *
    levelFactor *
    pflegegradFactor *
    regionFactor *
    ageFactor *
    diagnosisFactor *
    seasonFactor;

  const tf = normalizeTimeFactors(service.hours, service.timeFactors);
  const premiumSum = tf.evening + tf.night + tf.weekend + tf.holiday;
  const regularHours = Math.max(0, service.hours - premiumSum);

  const regularCost = regularHours * adjustedRate;
  const eveningCost = tf.evening * adjustedRate * 1.2;
  const nightCost = tf.night * adjustedRate * 1.5;
  const weekendCost = tf.weekend * adjustedRate * 1.2;
  const holidayCost = tf.holiday * adjustedRate * 1.5;

  const baseCost = regularCost + eveningCost + nightCost + weekendCost + holidayCost;

  const withSocial     = baseCost * (1 + SOCIAL_CONTRIB);
  const withVacation   = withSocial * (1 + VACATION_SICK);
  const withAdditional = withVacation * (1 + ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS);
  const withAdmin      = withAdditional * (1 + ADMINISTRATION);
  const withFixed      = withAdmin + (service.hours * FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR);

  return {
    baseCost,
    socialContributions: baseCost * SOCIAL_CONTRIB,
    vacationSick:        withSocial * VACATION_SICK,
    additionalPayments:  withVacation * ADDITIONAL_PAYMENTS,
    administration:      withAdditional * ADMINISTRATION,
    fixedCosts:          service.hours * FIXED_COSTS_PER_HOUR,
    totalCost:           withFixed,
    hourlyRate:          service.hours &gt; 0 ? withFixed / service.hours : 0,
    adjustedRate,
    factors: {
      complexity,
      level: levelFactor,
      pflegegrad: pflegegradFactor,
      region: regionFactor,
      age: ageFactor,
      diagnosis: diagnosisFactor,
      season: seasonFactor
    }
  };
};
```

## `src/features/pbc/storage.ts`
```ts
import type { ClientInfo, ClientStored, Scenario, Service, SettingsState } from &#x27;./types&#x27;;

const NS = &#x27;pbc.v1.&#x27;;
const KEY = (k: string) =&gt; NS + k;

export type PersistedShape = {
  version: 1;
  savedAt: string;
  services: Service[];
  clients: ClientStored[];
  clientInfo: ClientInfo;
  scenarios: Scenario[];
  settings: SettingsState;
};

export const saveJSON = (k: string, v: unknown) =&gt; {
  try { localStorage.setItem(KEY(k), JSON.stringify(v)); } catch {}
};

export const loadJSON = &lt;T&gt;(k: string, fallback: T): T =&gt; {
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(KEY(k));
    return raw ? (JSON.parse(raw) as T) : fallback;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
};

export const clearAll = () =&gt; {
  try {
    Object.keys(localStorage)
      .filter(k =&gt; k.startsWith(NS))
      .forEach(k =&gt; localStorage.removeItem(k));
  } catch {}
};

export const exportAll = (shape: Omit&lt;PersistedShape, &#x27;version&#x27; | &#x27;savedAt&#x27;&gt;) =&gt; {
  const payload: PersistedShape = {
    version: 1,
    savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    ...shape
  };
  return JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2);
};

export const importAll = (json: string) =&gt; {
  const data = JSON.parse(json) as PersistedShape;
  if (!data || data.version !== 1) throw new Error(&#x27;Unsupported JSON version&#x27;);
  saveJSON(&#x27;services&#x27;, data.services);
  saveJSON(&#x27;clients&#x27;, data.clients);
  saveJSON(&#x27;clientInfo&#x27;, data.clientInfo);
  saveJSON(&#x27;scenarios&#x27;, data.scenarios);
  saveJSON(&#x27;settings&#x27;, data.settings);
};

export const loadAllOrDefaults = &lt;TDefaults extends {
  services: Service[];
  clients: ClientStored[];
  clientInfo: ClientInfo;
  scenarios: Scenario[];
  settings: SettingsState;
}&gt;(defaults: TDefaults): TDefaults =&gt; {
  return {
    services: loadJSON(&#x27;services&#x27;, defaults.services),
    clients: loadJSON(&#x27;clients&#x27;, defaults.clients),
    clientInfo: loadJSON(&#x27;clientInfo&#x27;, defaults.clientInfo),
    scenarios: loadJSON(&#x27;scenarios&#x27;, defaults.scenarios),
    settings: loadJSON(&#x27;settings&#x27;, defaults.settings),
  } as TDefaults;
};
```

```tsx
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from &#x27;react&#x27;;

/** =========================
 *       Component
 *  ========================= */

const PersonalBudgetCalculator: React.FC = () =&gt; {
  /** Defaults (при первом запуске) */

  const defaultTotals: Totals = {
    baseCost: 0, socialContributions: 0, vacationSick: 0,
    additionalPayments: 0, administration: 0, fixedCosts: 0,
    totalCost: 0, totalHours: 0, averageHourlyRate: 0
  };

  const defaultClient: ClientInfo = {
    name: &#x27;&#x27;, birthDate: &#x27;&#x27;, diagnosis: &#x27;&#x27;, icfCodes: &#x27;&#x27;, address: &#x27;&#x27;, id: null
  };

  const defaultSettings: SettingsState = {
    autoSave: true, notifications: true, defaultRegion: &#x27;dresden&#x27;, currency: &#x27;EUR&#x27;, theme: &#x27;light&#x27;
  };

  /** Инициализация из localStorage */
  const loaded = loadAllOrDefaults({
    services: [defaultService],
    clients: [] as ClientStored[],
    clientInfo: defaultClient,
    scenarios: [] as Scenario[],
    settings: defaultSettings
  });

  const [services, setServices] = useState&lt;Service[]&gt;(loaded.services);
  const [clients, setClients] = useState&lt;ClientStored[]&gt;(loaded.clients);
  const [clientInfo, setClientInfo] = useState&lt;ClientInfo&gt;(loaded.clientInfo);
  const [scenarios, setScenarios] = useState&lt;Scenario[]&gt;(loaded.scenarios);
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState&lt;SettingsState&gt;(loaded.settings);

  const [totalCalculation, setTotalCalculation] = useState&lt;Totals&gt;(defaultTotals);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState&lt;&#x27;calculator&#x27; | &#x27;analytics&#x27; | &#x27;client&#x27; | &#x27;documents&#x27; | &#x27;scenarios&#x27; | &#x27;settings&#x27;&gt;(&#x27;calculator&#x27;);
  const [showAdvancedOptions, setShowAdvancedOptions] = useState(false);
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState&lt;Lang&gt;(&#x27;ru&#x27;);

  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState&lt;{ id: number; message: string; timestamp: string; read: boolean }[]&gt;([]);

  /** ——— i18n ——— */
  const t = (key: keyof typeof translations.ru) =&gt; translations[language][key] || key;

  /** ——— Notifications ——— */
  const addNotification = (message: string) =&gt; {
    const n = { id: Date.now(), message, timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), read: false };
    setNotifications(prev =&gt; [n, ...prev.slice(0, 9)]);
  };

  /** ——— Services ops ——— */
  const addService = () =&gt; {
    const newService: Service = {
      id: Date.now(),
      type: &#x27;dosug&#x27;,
      hours: 20,
      level: &#x27;mittel&#x27;,
      pflegegrad: &#x27;pg3&#x27;,
      region: settings.defaultRegion,
      ageGroup: &#x27;adult&#x27;,
      diagnosis: &#x27;physical&#x27;,
      season: &#x27;standard&#x27;,
      timeFactors: { evening: 0, night: 0, weekend: 0, holiday: 0 }
    };
    setServices(prev =&gt; [...prev, newService]);
  };

  const removeService = (id: number) =&gt; {
    setServices(prev =&gt; prev.filter(s =&gt; s.id !== id));
  };

  const updateService = &lt;K extends keyof Service&gt;(id: number, field: K, value: Service[K]) =&gt; {
    setServices(prev =&gt;
```
